I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[cli-tools-test] audit: tool_types=0 for Copilot engine runs despite MCP tool usage
### Problem Description

When auditing a completed workflow run using the Copilot engine, the behavior fingerprint reports `tool_types: 0` and `tool_breadth: "narrow"` even when MCP tools were clearly used. The `observability_insights` section echoes this incorrect value: _"The agent used 20 turns across 0 tool types"_.

This produces a misleading analysis since the same run's `mcp_tool_usage` section correctly records tool calls (e.g., `safeoutputs.create_discussion`, `safeoutputs.push_repo_memory`).

By contrast, auditing a Claude engine run (same test session) correctly shows `tool_types: 4` and `tool_breadth: "moderate"`.

### Tool

- **Tool**: `audit` (agentic-workflows MCP server)
- **Engine affected**: `copilot` (Claude engine is unaffected)

### Steps to Reproduce

1. Run any Copilot engine workflow that calls MCP tools (e.g., `safeoutputs.create_discussion`)
2. Audit the completed run:
   ```
   audit(run_id_or_url: "<copilot-run-id>")
   ```
3. Check `behavior_fingerprint.tool_types` and `observability_insights` in the response

### Expected Behavior

`tool_types` should reflect the number of distinct MCP tool types actually invoked during the run. For a run that used `safeoutputs.create_discussion` and `safeoutputs.push_repo_memory`, the value should be at least `1` (one MCP server) or `2` (two distinct tool names).

### Actual Behavior

```json
{
  "behavior_fingerprint": {
    "tool_breadth": "narrow",
    "tool_types": 0
  },
  "observability_insights": [
    {
      "summary": "The agent used 20 turns across 0 tool types ..."
    }
  ]
}
```

Meanwhile the same audit shows `mcp_tool_usage.summary` with:
```json
[
  {"server_name": "safeoutputs", "tool_name": "create_discussion", "call_count": 1},
  {"server_name": "safeoutputs", "tool_name": "push_repo_memory",  "call_count": 2}
]
```

### Evidence

- **Affected run**: [§24493327785](https://github.com/github/gh-aw/actions/runs/24493327785) — "Copilot PR Prompt Pattern Analysis", engine `copilot` v1.0.21, 20 turns, 3 MCP tool calls
- **Unaffected run**: [§24493292984](https://github.com/github/gh-aw/actions/runs/24493292984) — "Design Decision Gate", engine `claude`, 5 turns → `tool_types: 4` ✅
- **Test session run**: [§24493738931](https://github.com/github/gh-aw/actions/runs/24493738931)

### Root Cause (Hypothesis)

The `tool_types` counter likely parses tool call events from Claude-format agent logs. Copilot engine runs may use a different log format where tool invocations are not attributed as individual typed events, causing the counter to remain at `0` even when `mcp_tool_usage` has correct data from a separate parsing path.

### Impact

- **Severity**: Medium
- **Frequency**: Affects every Copilot engine run audit
- **Workaround**: Ignore `behavior_fingerprint.tool_breadth` / `tool_types`; use `mcp_tool_usage.summary` directly for tool usage analysis

### Additional Context

Also observed during this test session:

1. **`github-agentic-workflows` MCP server fails in Design Decision Gate** — The server shows status `"failed"` with 0 requests in run [§24493292984](https://github.com/github/gh-aw/actions/runs/24493292984). The workflow completed successfully without it, suggesting it is configured but unused, yet it adds noise to the audit report and contributes to the "capability friction" warning.

2. **`logs` tool file path is inaccessible** — The `logs` MCP tool response includes `"Use the file_path to read the full data"` pointing to `/tmp/gh-aw/logs-cache/<hash>.json`, but that directory is owned by `root:root` with mode `0700` and cannot be read by the workflow agent user. The equivalent data is available via per-run `run_summary.json` files in `/tmp/gh-aw/aw-mcp/logs/`, but the message is confusing.

    15	var auditAgenticLog = logger.New("cli:audit_agentic_analysis")

    17	// TaskDomainInfo describes the dominant task type inferred for a workflow run.
    18	type TaskDomainInfo struct {
    19	        Name   string `json:"name"`
    20	        Label  string `json:"label"`
    21	        Reason string `json:"reason,omitempty"`
    22	}
    23	
    24	// BehaviorFingerprint summarizes the run's execution profile in compact dimensions.
    25	type BehaviorFingerprint struct {
    26	        ExecutionStyle  string  `json:"execution_style"`
    27	        ToolBreadth     string  `json:"tool_breadth"`
    28	        ActuationStyle  string  `json:"actuation_style"`
    29	        ResourceProfile string  `json:"resource_profile"`
    30	        DispatchMode    string  `json:"dispatch_mode"`
    31	        AgenticFraction float64 `json:"agentic_fraction"` // Ratio of reasoning turns to total turns (0.0-1.0)
    32	}

    34	// AgenticAssessment captures an actionable judgment about the run's behavior.

    36	        Kind           string `json:"kind"`

    43	func buildToolUsageInfo(metrics LogMetrics) []ToolUsageInfo {
    44	        toolStats := make(map[string]*ToolUsageInfo)
    45	
    46	        for _, toolCall := range metrics.ToolCalls {
    47	                displayKey := workflow.PrettifyToolName(toolCall.Name)
    48	                if existing, exists := toolStats[displayKey]; exists {
    49	                        existing.CallCount += toolCall.CallCount
    50	                        if toolCall.MaxInputSize > existing.MaxInputSize {
    51	                                existing.MaxInputSize = toolCall.MaxInputSize
    52	                        }
    53	                        if toolCall.MaxOutputSize > existing.MaxOutputSize {
    54	                                existing.MaxOutputSize = toolCall.MaxOutputSize
    55	                        }
    56	                        if toolCall.MaxDuration > 0 {
    57	                                maxDuration := timeutil.FormatDuration(toolCall.MaxDuration)
    58	                                if existing.MaxDuration == "" || toolCall.MaxDuration > parseDurationString(existing.MaxDuration) {
    59	                                        existing.MaxDuration = maxDuration
    60	                                }
    61	                        }
    62	                        continue
    63	                }
    64	
    65	                info := &ToolUsageInfo{
    66	                        Name:          displayKey,
    67	                        CallCount:     toolCall.CallCount,
    68	                        MaxInputSize:  toolCall.MaxInputSize,
    69	                        MaxOutputSize: toolCall.MaxOutputSize,
    70	                }
    71	                if toolCall.MaxDuration > 0 {
    72	                        info.MaxDuration = timeutil.FormatDuration(toolCall.MaxDuration)
    73	                }
    74	                toolStats[displayKey] = info
    75	        }
    76	
    77	        toolUsage := make([]ToolUsageInfo, 0, len(toolStats))
    78	        for _, info := range toolStats {
    79	                toolUsage = append(toolUsage, *info)
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        slices.SortFunc(toolUsage, func(a, b ToolUsageInfo) int {
    83	                if a.CallCount != b.CallCount {
    84	                        return b.CallCount - a.CallCount
    85	                }
    86	                return strings.Compare(a.Name, b.Name)
    87	        })
    88	
    89	        return toolUsage
    90	}

    92	func deriveRunAgenticAnalysis(processedRun ProcessedRun, metrics LogMetrics) (*AwContext, []ToolUsageInfo, []CreatedItemReport, *TaskDomainInfo, *BehaviorFingerprint, []AgenticAssessment) {
    93	        auditAgenticLog.Printf("Deriving agentic analysis for run: id=%d workflow=%s", processedRun.Run.DatabaseID, processedRun.Run.WorkflowName)
    94	        var awContext *AwContext
    95	        if processedRun.AwContext != nil {
    96	                awContext = processedRun.AwContext
    97	        } else if processedRun.Run.LogsPath != "" {
    98	                awInfoPath := filepath.Join(processedRun.Run.LogsPath, "aw_info.json")
    99	                if info, err := parseAwInfo(awInfoPath, false); err == nil && info != nil {
   100	                        awContext = info.Context
   101	                }
   102	        }
   103	
   104	        toolUsage := buildToolUsageInfo(metrics)
   105	        createdItems := extractCreatedItemsFromManifest(processedRun.Run.LogsPath)
   106	        metricsData := MetricsData{
   107	                TokenUsage:    processedRun.Run.TokenUsage,
   108	                EstimatedCost: processedRun.Run.EstimatedCost,
   109	                ActionMinutes: processedRun.Run.ActionMinutes,
   110	                Turns:         processedRun.Run.Turns,
   111	                ErrorCount:    processedRun.Run.ErrorCount,
   112	                WarningCount:  processedRun.Run.WarningCount,
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        taskDomain := detectTaskDomain(processedRun, createdItems, toolUsage, awContext)
   116	        behaviorFingerprint := buildBehaviorFingerprint(processedRun, metricsData, toolUsage, createdItems, awContext)
   117	        agenticAssessments := buildAgenticAssessments(processedRun, metricsData, toolUsage, createdItems, taskDomain, behaviorFingerprint, awContext)
   118	
   119	        auditAgenticLog.Printf("Agentic analysis complete: tool_types=%d created_items=%d assessments=%d", len(toolUsage), len(createdItems), len(agenticAssessments))
   120	        return awContext, toolUsage, createdItems, taskDomain, behaviorFingerprint, agenticAssessments
   121	}
   122	
   123	func detectTaskDomain(processedRun ProcessedRun, createdItems []CreatedItemReport, toolUsage []ToolUsageInfo, awContext *AwContext) *TaskDomainInfo {
   124	        auditAgenticLog.Printf("Detecting task domain for run: workflow=%s event=%s", processedRun.Run.WorkflowName, processedRun.Run.Event)
   125	        combined := strings.ToLower(strings.Join([]string{
   126	                processedRun.Run.WorkflowName,
   127	                processedRun.Run.WorkflowPath,
   128	                processedRun.Run.Event,
   129	        }, " "))
   130	
   131	        createdTypes := make([]string, 0, len(createdItems))
   132	        for _, item := range createdItems {
   133	                createdTypes = append(createdTypes, strings.ToLower(item.Type))
   134	        }
   135	        createdJoined := strings.Join(createdTypes, " ")
   136	
   137	        toolNames := make([]string, 0, len(toolUsage))
   138	        for _, tool := range toolUsage {
   139	                toolNames = append(toolNames, strings.ToLower(tool.Name))
   140	        }
   141	        toolJoined := strings.Join(toolNames, " ")
   142	
   143	        switch {
   144	        case containsAny(combined, "release", "deploy", "publish", "backport", "changelog"):
   145	                return &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "release_ops", Label: "Release / Ops", Reason: "Workflow metadata matches release or operational automation."}
   146	        case containsAny(combined, "research", "investigat", "analysis", "analy", "report", "audit"):
   147	                return &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "research", Label: "Research", Reason: "Workflow naming and instructions suggest exploratory analysis or reporting."}
   148	        case containsAny(combined, "triage", "label", "classif", "route") || containsAny(createdJoined, "add_labels", "remove_labels", "set_issue_type"):
   149	                return &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "triage", Label: "Triage", Reason: "The run focused on classification, routing, or issue state updates."}
   150	        case containsAny(combined, "fix", "patch", "repair", "refactor", "swe", "code", "review") || containsAny(createdJoined, "create_pull_request_review_comment", "submit_pull_request_review"):
   151	                return &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "code_fix", Label: "Code Fix", Reason: "The workflow appears oriented toward code changes or pull request review."}
   152	        case containsAny(combined, "cleanup", "maint", "update", "deps", "sync", "housekeeping"):
   153	                return &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "repo_maintenance", Label: "Repo Maintenance", Reason: "Workflow metadata matches repository maintenance or update work."}
   154	        case containsAny(combined, "issue", "discussion", "comment", "support", "reply") || containsAny(createdJoined, "add_comment", "create_discussion"):
   155	                return &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "issue_response", Label: "Issue Response", Reason: "The run is primarily interacting with issue, discussion, or comment threads."}
   156	        case awContext != nil:
   157	                return &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "delegated_automation", Label: "Delegated Automation", Reason: "The run was dispatched from an upstream workflow and is acting as a delegated task."}
   158	        case containsAny(toolJoined, "github_issue_read", "github-discussion-query"):
   159	                return &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "issue_response", Label: "Issue Response", Reason: "Tool usage centers on repository conversations and issue context."}
   160	        default:
   161	                return &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "general_automation", Label: "General Automation", Reason: "The run does not strongly match a narrower workflow domain yet."}
   162	        }
   163	}
   164	
   165	func buildBehaviorFingerprint(processedRun ProcessedRun, metrics MetricsData, toolUsage []ToolUsageInfo, createdItems []CreatedItemReport, awContext *AwContext) *BehaviorFingerprint {
   166	        auditAgenticLog.Printf("Building behavior fingerprint: run_id=%d turns=%d tool_types=%d created_items=%d", processedRun.Run.DatabaseID, metrics.Turns, len(toolUsage), len(createdItems))
   167	        toolTypes := len(toolUsage)
   168	        writeCount := len(createdItems) + processedRun.Run.SafeItemsCount
   169	
   170	        executionStyle := "directed"
   171	        switch {
   172	        case metrics.Turns >= 10 || toolTypes >= 6:
   173	                executionStyle = "exploratory"
   174	        case metrics.Turns >= 5 || toolTypes >= 4:
   175	                executionStyle = "adaptive"
   176	        }
   177	
   178	        toolBreadth := "narrow"
   179	        switch {
   180	        case toolTypes >= 6:
   181	                toolBreadth = "broad"
   182	        case toolTypes >= 3:
   183	                toolBreadth = "moderate"
   184	        }
   185	
   186	        actuationStyle := "read_only"
   187	        switch {
   188	        case writeCount >= 6:
   189	                actuationStyle = "write_heavy"
   190	        case writeCount > 0:
   191	                actuationStyle = "selective_write"
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        resourceProfile := "lean"
   195	        switch {
   196	        case processedRun.Run.Duration >= 15*time.Minute || metrics.Turns >= 12 || toolTypes >= 6 || writeCount >= 8:
   197	                resourceProfile = "heavy"
   198	        case processedRun.Run.Duration >= 5*time.Minute || metrics.Turns >= 6 || toolTypes >= 4 || writeCount >= 3:
   199	                resourceProfile = "moderate"
   200	        }
   201	
   202	        dispatchMode := "standalone"
   203	        if awContext != nil {
   204	                dispatchMode = "delegated"
   205	        }
   206	
   207	        agenticFraction := computeAgenticFraction(processedRun)
   208	
   209	        auditAgenticLog.Printf("Behavior fingerprint: execution=%s breadth=%s actuation=%s resource=%s dispatch=%s agentic_fraction=%.2f", executionStyle, toolBreadth, actuationStyle, resourceProfile, dispatchMode, agenticFraction)
   210	        return &BehaviorFingerprint{
   211	                ExecutionStyle:  executionStyle,
   212	                ToolBreadth:     toolBreadth,
   213	                ActuationStyle:  actuationStyle,
   214	                ResourceProfile: resourceProfile,
   215	                DispatchMode:    dispatchMode,
   216	                AgenticFraction: agenticFraction,
   217	        }
   218	}
   219	
   220	func buildAgenticAssessments(processedRun ProcessedRun, metrics MetricsData, toolUsage []ToolUsageInfo, createdItems []CreatedItemReport, domain *TaskDomainInfo, fingerprint *BehaviorFingerprint, awContext *AwContext) []AgenticAssessment {
   221	        if domain == nil || fingerprint == nil {
   222	                auditAgenticLog.Print("Skipping agentic assessments: missing domain or fingerprint")
   223	                return nil
   224	        }
   225	        auditAgenticLog.Printf("Building agentic assessments: run_id=%d domain=%s resource=%s execution=%s", processedRun.Run.DatabaseID, domain.Name, fingerprint.ResourceProfile, fingerprint.ExecutionStyle)
   226	
   227	        assessments := make([]AgenticAssessment, 0, 4)
   228	        toolTypes := len(toolUsage)
   229	        frictionEvents := len(processedRun.MissingTools) + len(processedRun.MCPFailures) + len(processedRun.MissingData)
   230	        writeCount := len(createdItems) + processedRun.Run.SafeItemsCount
   231	
   232	        if fingerprint.ResourceProfile == "heavy" {
   233	                severity := "medium"
   234	                if metrics.Turns >= 14 || toolTypes >= 7 || processedRun.Run.Duration >= 20*time.Minute {
   235	                        severity = "high"
   236	                }
   237	                assessments = append(assessments, AgenticAssessment{
   238	                        Kind:           "resource_heavy_for_domain",
   239	                        Severity:       severity,
   240	                        Summary:        fmt.Sprintf("This %s run consumed a heavy execution profile for its task shape.", domain.Label),
   241	                        Evidence:       fmt.Sprintf("turns=%d tool_types=%d duration=%s write_actions=%d", metrics.Turns, toolTypes, formatAssessmentDuration(processedRun.Run.Duration), writeCount),
   242	                        Recommendation: "Compare this run to similar successful runs and trim unnecessary turns, tools, or write actions.",
   243	                })
   244	        }
   245	
   246	        if (domain.Name == "triage" || domain.Name == "repo_maintenance" || domain.Name == "issue_response") && fingerprint.ResourceProfile == "lean" && fingerprint.ExecutionStyle == "directed" && fingerprint.ToolBreadth == "narrow" {
   247	                assessments = append(assessments, AgenticAssessment{
   248	                        Kind:           "overkill_for_agentic",
   249	                        Severity:       "low",
   250	                        Summary:        fmt.Sprintf("This %s run looks stable enough that deterministic automation may be a simpler fit.", domain.Label),
   251	                        Evidence:       fmt.Sprintf("turns=%d tool_types=%d actuation=%s", metrics.Turns, toolTypes, fingerprint.ActuationStyle),
   252	                        Recommendation: "Consider whether a scripted rule or deterministic workflow step could replace this agentic path.",
   253	                })
   254	        }
   255	
   256	        if frictionEvents >= 3 || (frictionEvents > 0 && writeCount >= 3) || ((domain.Name == "triage" || domain.Name == "repo_maintenance" || domain.Name == "issue_response") && fingerprint.ExecutionStyle == "exploratory") {
   257	                severity := "medium"
   258	                if frictionEvents >= 4 || (frictionEvents > 0 && fingerprint.ActuationStyle == "write_heavy") {
   259	                        severity = "high"
   260	                }
   261	                assessments = append(assessments, AgenticAssessment{
   262	                        Kind:           "poor_agentic_control",
   263	                        Severity:       severity,
   264	                        Summary:        "The run showed signs of broad or weakly controlled agentic behavior.",
   265	                        Evidence:       fmt.Sprintf("friction=%d execution=%s actuation=%s", frictionEvents, fingerprint.ExecutionStyle, fingerprint.ActuationStyle),
   266	                        Recommendation: "Tighten instructions, reduce unnecessary tools, or delay write actions until the workflow has stronger evidence.",
   267	                })
   268	        }
   269	
   270	        // Partially reducible: the workflow has a low agentic fraction, meaning
   271	        // many turns are data-gathering that could be moved to deterministic steps:
   272	        // or post-steps: in the frontmatter. Only flag when there's substantive work
   273	        // (not lean/directed runs which overkill_for_agentic already covers).
   274	        if fingerprint.AgenticFraction > 0 && fingerprint.AgenticFraction < 0.6 &&
   275	                fingerprint.ResourceProfile != "lean" {
   276	                severity := "low"
   277	                if fingerprint.AgenticFraction < 0.4 {
   278	                        severity = "medium"
   279	                }
   280	                deterministicPct := int((1.0 - fingerprint.AgenticFraction) * 100)
   281	                assessments = append(assessments, AgenticAssessment{
   282	                        Kind:           "partially_reducible",
   283	                        Severity:       severity,
   284	                        Summary:        fmt.Sprintf("About %d%% of this run's turns appear to be data-gathering that could move to deterministic steps.", deterministicPct),
   285	                        Evidence:       fmt.Sprintf("agentic_fraction=%.2f turns=%d", fingerprint.AgenticFraction, metrics.Turns),
   286	                        Recommendation: "Move data-fetching work to frontmatter steps: (pre-agent) writing to /tmp/gh-aw/agent/ or post-steps: (post-agent) to reduce inference cost. See the Deterministic & Agentic Patterns guide.",
   287	                })
   288	        }
   289	
   290	        // Model downgrade suggestion: the run uses a heavy resource profile but
   291	        // the task domain is simple enough that a smaller model would likely suffice.
   292	        if fingerprint.ResourceProfile != "lean" &&
   293	                (domain.Name == "triage" || domain.Name == "repo_maintenance" || domain.Name == "issue_response") &&
   294	                fingerprint.ActuationStyle != "write_heavy" {
   295	                assessments = append(assessments, AgenticAssessment{
   296	                        Kind:           "model_downgrade_available",
   297	                        Severity:       "low",
   298	                        Summary:        fmt.Sprintf("This %s run may not need a frontier model. A smaller model (e.g. gpt-4.1-mini, claude-haiku-4-5) could handle the task at lower cost.", domain.Label),
   299	                        Evidence:       fmt.Sprintf("domain=%s resource_profile=%s actuation=%s", domain.Name, fingerprint.ResourceProfile, fingerprint.ActuationStyle),
   300	                        Recommendation: "Try engine.model: gpt-4.1-mini or claude-haiku-4-5 in the workflow frontmatter.",
   301	                })
   302	        }
   303	
   304	        if awContext != nil {
   305	                assessments = append(assessments, AgenticAssessment{
   306	                        Kind:           "delegated_context_present",
   307	                        Severity:       "info",
   308	                        Summary:        "The run preserved upstream dispatch context, which helps trace multi-workflow episodes.",
   309	                        Evidence:       fmt.Sprintf("workflow_call_id=%s event_type=%s", awContext.WorkflowCallID, awContext.EventType),
   310	                        Recommendation: "Use this context when comparing downstream runs so follow-up workflows are evaluated as part of one task chain.",
   311	                })
   312	        }
   313	
   314	        auditAgenticLog.Printf("Built %d agentic assessments", len(assessments))
   315	        return assessments
   316	}
   317

    28	        BatchSize = 100
    29	        // BatchSizeForAllWorkflows is the larger batch size when searching for agentic workflows
    30	        // There can be a really large number of workflow runs in a repository, so
    31	        // we are generous in the batch size when used without qualification.
    32	        BatchSizeForAllWorkflows = 250
    33	        // MaxConcurrentDownloads limits the number of parallel artifact downloads

    35	        // APICallCooldown is the minimum pause between successive batch-fetch iterations to
    36	        // avoid hitting the GitHub API rate limit when processing many runs in a single
    37	        // invocation.  checkAndWaitForRateLimit always sleeps at least this long.
    38	        APICallCooldown = 500 * time.Millisecond

    42	        // window so subsequent iterations are not rejected with a 403/429.

   186	// RunSummary represents a complete summary of a workflow run's artifacts and metrics.
   187	// This file is written to each run folder as "run_summary.json" to cache processing results
   188	// and avoid re-downloading and re-processing already analyzed runs.
   189	//
   190	// Key features:
   191	// - Acts as a marker that a run has been fully processed
   192	// - Stores all extracted metrics and analysis results
   193	// - Includes CLI version for cache invalidation when the tool is updated
   194	// - Enables fast reloading of run data without re-parsing logs
   195	//
   196	// Cache invalidation:
   197	// - If the CLI version in the summary doesn't match the current version, the run is reprocessed
   198	// - This ensures that bug fixes and improvements in log parsing are automatically applied
   199	type RunSummary struct {
   200	        CLIVersion              string                   `json:"cli_version"`                       // CLI version used to process this run
   201	        RunID                   int64                    `json:"run_id"`                            // Workflow run database ID
   202	        ProcessedAt             time.Time                `json:"processed_at"`                      // When this summary was created
   203	        Run                     WorkflowRun              `json:"run"`                               // Full workflow run metadata
   204	        Metrics                 LogMetrics               `json:"metrics"`                           // Extracted log metrics
   205	        AwContext               *AwContext               `json:"context,omitempty"`                 // aw_context data from aw_info.json
   206	        TaskDomain              *TaskDomainInfo          `json:"task_domain,omitempty"`             // Inferred workflow task domain
   207	        BehaviorFingerprint     *BehaviorFingerprint     `json:"behavior_fingerprint,omitempty"`    // Compact execution profile
   208	        AgenticAssessments      []AgenticAssessment      `json:"agentic_assessments,omitempty"`     // Derived agentic judgments
   209	        AccessAnalysis          *DomainAnalysis          `json:"access_analysis"`                   // Network access analysis
   210	        FirewallAnalysis        *FirewallAnalysis        `json:"firewall_analysis"`                 // Firewall log analysis
   211	        PolicyAnalysis          *PolicyAnalysis          `json:"policy_analysis,omitempty"`         // Firewall policy rule attribution
   212	        RedactedDomainsAnalysis *RedactedDomainsAnalysis `json:"redacted_domains_analysis"`         // Redacted URL domains analysis
   213	        MissingTools            []MissingToolReport      `json:"missing_tools"`                     // Missing tool reports
   214	        MissingData             []MissingDataReport      `json:"missing_data"`                      // Missing data reports
   215	        Noops                   []NoopReport             `json:"noops"`                             // Noop messages
   216	        MCPFailures             []MCPFailureReport       `json:"mcp_failures"`                      // MCP server failures
   217	        MCPToolUsage            *MCPToolUsageData        `json:"mcp_tool_usage,omitempty"`          // MCP tool usage data
   218	        TokenUsage              *TokenUsageSummary       `json:"token_usage_summary,omitempty"`     // Token usage from firewall proxy
   219	        GitHubRateLimitUsage    *GitHubRateLimitUsage    `json:"github_rate_limit_usage,omitempty"` // GitHub API quota consumption

   269	// AwContext represents the caller-workflow identity injected by dispatch_workflow.cjs
   270	// into the aw_context input, and stored under the "context" key in aw_info.json.
   271	// All values are strings (no nested objects) as validated by generate_aw_info.cjs.
   272	type AwContext struct {
   273	        Repo           string `json:"repo"`                       // "owner/repo" of the calling workflow
   274	        RunID          string `json:"run_id"`                     // GitHub Actions run ID of the calling workflow
   275	        WorkflowID     string `json:"workflow_id"`                // Full workflow ref, e.g. "owner/repo/.github/workflows/foo.yml@refs/heads/main"
   276	        WorkflowCallID string `json:"workflow_call_id,omitempty"` // Unique call attempt ID (run_id + run_attempt)
   277	        Time           string `json:"time,omitempty"`             // ISO 8601 timestamp of the dispatch
   278	        Actor          string `json:"actor,omitempty"`            // GitHub actor that triggered the calling workflow
   279	        EventType      string `json:"event_type,omitempty"`       // GitHub event name of the calling workflow
   280	        ItemType       string `json:"item_type,omitempty"`        // Kind of triggering item: "issue", "pull_request", "discussion", "check_run", "check_suite", or ""
   281	        ItemNumber     string `json:"item_number,omitempty"`      // Number (issue/PR/discussion) or database id (check_run/check_suite) of the triggering item
   282	        CommentID      string `json:"comment_id,omitempty"`       // ID of the triggering comment or review; empty when not a comment/review event
   283	}

   238	// buildAuditData creates structured audit data from workflow run information
   239	func buildAuditData(processedRun ProcessedRun, metrics LogMetrics, mcpToolUsage *MCPToolUsageData) AuditData {
   240	        run := processedRun.Run
   241	        auditReportLog.Printf("Building audit data for run ID %d", run.DatabaseID)
   242	
   243	        // Build overview
   244	        overview := OverviewData{
   245	                RunID:        run.DatabaseID,
   246	                WorkflowName: run.WorkflowName,
   247	                Status:       run.Status,
   248	                Conclusion:   run.Conclusion,
   249	                CreatedAt:    run.CreatedAt,
   250	                StartedAt:    run.StartedAt,
   251	                UpdatedAt:    run.UpdatedAt,
   252	                Event:        run.Event,
   253	                Branch:       run.HeadBranch,
   254	                URL:          run.URL,
   255	        }
   256	
   257	        if run.LogsPath != "" {
   258	                overview.LogsPath = run.LogsPath
   259	        }
   260	
   261	        if run.Duration > 0 {
   262	                overview.Duration = timeutil.FormatDuration(run.Duration)
   263	        }
   264	
   265	        if run.LogsPath != "" {
   266	                awInfoPath := filepath.Join(run.LogsPath, "aw_info.json")
   267	                if awInfo, err := parseAwInfo(awInfoPath, false); err == nil && awInfo != nil {
   268	                        overview.AwContext = awInfo.Context
   269	                }
   270	        }
   271	
   272	        // Build metrics
   273	        metricsData := MetricsData{
   274	                TokenUsage:    run.TokenUsage,
   275	                EstimatedCost: run.EstimatedCost,
   276	                Turns:         run.Turns,
   277	                ErrorCount:    run.ErrorCount,
   278	                WarningCount:  run.WarningCount,
   279	        }
   280	
   281	        // Populate effective tokens from the firewall proxy summary when available,
   282	        // otherwise fall back to the effective tokens stored on the run itself.
   283	        if processedRun.TokenUsage != nil && processedRun.TokenUsage.TotalEffectiveTokens > 0 {
   284	                metricsData.EffectiveTokens = processedRun.TokenUsage.TotalEffectiveTokens
   285	        } else if run.EffectiveTokens > 0 {
   286	                metricsData.EffectiveTokens = run.EffectiveTokens
   287	        }
   288	
   289	        // Populate ActionMinutes from run duration so it is always visible even
   290	        // when token/turn metrics are zero (e.g. Codex runs that exit early).

   389	// extractDownloadedFiles scans the logs directory and returns file information
   390	func extractDownloadedFiles(logsPath string) []FileInfo {
   391	        auditReportLog.Printf("Extracting downloaded files from: %s", logsPath)
   392	        var files []FileInfo
   393	
   394	        entries, err := os.ReadDir(logsPath)
   395	        if err != nil {
   396	                auditReportLog.Printf("Failed to read logs directory: %v", err)
   397	                return files
   398	        }
   399	
   400	        for _, entry := range entries {
   401	                // Skip directories
   402	                if entry.IsDir() {
   403	                        continue
   404	                }
   405	
   406	                name := entry.Name()
   407	                fullPath := filepath.Join(logsPath, name)
   408	
   409	                // Use absolute path so callers get a directly usable path
   410	                absPath, err := filepath.Abs(fullPath)
   411	                if err != nil {
   412	                        auditReportLog.Printf("Failed to resolve absolute path for %s: %v", fullPath, err)
   413	                        absPath = fullPath
   414	                }
   415	
   416	                fileInfo := FileInfo{
   417	                        Path:        absPath,
   418	                        Description: describeFile(name),
   419	                }
   420

   489	// renderAuditReport builds and renders the audit report from a fully-populated processedRun.
   490	// It is called both when serving from a cached run summary and after a fresh processing pass,

   492	func renderAuditReport(ctx context.Context, processedRun ProcessedRun, metrics LogMetrics, mcpToolUsage *MCPToolUsageData, runOutputDir string, owner, repo, hostname string, verbose bool, parse bool, jsonOutput bool) error {

   494	
   495	        currentCreatedItems := extractCreatedItemsFromManifest(runOutputDir)
   496	        processedRun.Run.SafeItemsCount = len(currentCreatedItems)
   497	
   498	        currentSnapshot := buildAuditComparisonSnapshot(processedRun, currentCreatedItems)
   499	        comparison := buildAuditComparisonForRun(ctx, processedRun, currentSnapshot, runOutputDir, owner, repo, hostname, verbose)
   500	
   501	        // Build structured audit data
   502	        auditData := buildAuditData(processedRun, metrics, mcpToolUsage)
   503	        auditData.Comparison = comparison
   504	
   505	        // Render output based on format preference
   506	        if jsonOutput {
   507	                if err := renderJSON(auditData); err != nil {
   508	                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to render JSON output: %w", err)
   509	                }
   510	        } else {
   511	                renderConsole(auditData, runOutputDir)
   512	        }
   513	
   514	        // Display gateway metrics if available
   515	        if gatewayMetrics, err := parseGatewayLogs(runOutputDir, verbose); err == nil {
   516	                if metricsOutput := renderGatewayMetricsTable(gatewayMetrics, verbose); metricsOutput != "" {
   517	                        fmt.Fprint(os.Stderr, metricsOutput)
   518	                }
   519	        }

    12	
    13	var metricsLog = logger.New("workflow:metrics")
    14	
    15	// ToolCallInfo represents statistics for a single tool
    16	type ToolCallInfo struct {
    17	        Name          string        // Prettified tool name (e.g., "github::search_issues", "bash")
    18	        CallCount     int           // Number of times this tool was called
    19	        MaxInputSize  int           // Maximum input size in tokens for any call
    20	        MaxOutputSize int           // Maximum output size in tokens for any call
    21	        MaxDuration   time.Duration // Maximum execution duration for any call
    22	}
    23	
    24	// LogMetrics represents extracted metrics from log files
    25	type LogMetrics struct {
    26	        TokenUsage             int
    27	        EstimatedCost          float64
    28	        Turns                  int            // Number of turns needed to complete the task
    29	        ToolCalls              []ToolCallInfo // Tool call statistics
    30	        ToolSequences          [][]string     // Sequences of tool calls preserving order
    31	        AvgTimeBetweenTurns    time.Duration  // Mean time between consecutive LLM API calls (computed from per-turn timestamps when available)
    32	        MaxTimeBetweenTurns    time.Duration  // Maximum time between any two consecutive LLM API calls
    33	        MedianTimeBetweenTurns time.Duration  // Median time between consecutive LLM API calls
    34	        // StdDevTimeBetweenTurns is the sample standard deviation (Bessel's correction, n-1
    35	        // denominator) of inter-turn intervals, treating the observed turns as a sample of
    36	        // the agent's execution behaviour rather than an exhaustive population.
    37	        StdDevTimeBetweenTurns time.Duration
    38	        // Timestamp removed - use GitHub API timestamps instead of parsing from logs
    39	}
    40	
    41	// ExtractJSONMetrics extracts metrics from streaming JSON log lines
    42	func ExtractJSONMetrics(line string, verbose bool) LogMetrics {
    43	        var metrics LogMetrics
    44	
    45	        // Trim the line first
    46	        trimmed := strings.TrimSpace(line)
    47	        if trimmed == "" {
    48	                return metrics
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        metricsLog.Printf("Extracting metrics from JSON line: line_length=%d", len(trimmed))
    52	
    53	        // If the line isn't a clean JSON object, try to extract a JSON object substring
    54	        jsonStr := trimmed
    55	        if !strings.HasPrefix(trimmed, "{") || !strings.HasSuffix(trimmed, "}") {
    56	                // Find first '{' and last '}' and attempt to parse that slice
    57	                open := strings.Index(trimmed, "{")
    58	                close := strings.LastIndex(trimmed, "}")
    59	                if open == -1 || close == -1 || close <= open {
    60	                        return metrics
    61	                }
    62	                jsonStr = trimmed[open : close+1]
    63	        }
    64	
    65	        // Try to parse as generic JSON
    66	        var jsonData map[string]any
    67	        if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonStr), &jsonData); err != nil {
    68	                // If parsing fails, try a relaxed approach: sometimes logs contain a JSON-like object with single quotes
    69	                // Replace single quotes with double quotes as a last resort (not ideal, but helpful for noisy logs)
    70	                relaxed := strings.ReplaceAll(jsonStr, "'", "\"")

   340	// ValidateHeredocDelimiter checks that a delimiter is safe for use inside
   341	// single-quoted heredoc syntax (<< 'DELIM'). Rejects delimiters containing
   342	// single quotes, newlines, carriage returns, or non-printable characters
   343	// that could break the generated shell/YAML.
   344	func ValidateHeredocDelimiter(delimiter string) error {
   345	        for _, r := range delimiter {
   346	                switch {
   347	                case r == '\'':
   348	                        return fmt.Errorf("heredoc delimiter %q contains single quote", delimiter)
   349	                case r == '\n', r == '\r':
   350	                        return fmt.Errorf("heredoc delimiter %q contains newline", delimiter)
   351	                case r < 0x20 && r != '\t':
   352	                        return fmt.Errorf("heredoc delimiter %q contains non-printable character %U", delimiter, r)
   353	                }
   354	        }
   355	        return nil
   356	}
   357	
   358	// PrettifyToolName removes "mcp__" prefix and formats tool names nicely
   359	func PrettifyToolName(toolName string) string {
   360	        // Handle MCP tools: "mcp__github__search_issues" -> "github_search_issues"
   361	        // Avoid colons and leave underscores as-is
   362	        if strings.HasPrefix(toolName, "mcp__") {
   363	                parts := strings.Split(toolName, "__")
   364	                if len(parts) >= 3 {
   365	                        provider := parts[1]
   366	                        method := strings.Join(parts[2:], "_")
   367	                        return fmt.Sprintf("%s_%s", provider, method)
   368	                }
   369	                // If format is unexpected, just remove the mcp__ prefix
   370	                return strings.TrimPrefix(toolName, "mcp__")
   371	        }
   372	
   373	        // Handle bash specially - keep as "bash"
   374	        if strings.ToLower(toolName) == "bash" {
   375	                return "bash"
   376	        }
   377	
   378	        // Return other tool names as-is
   379	        return toolName
   380	}
   381	
   382	// SanitizeWorkflowIDForCacheKey sanitizes a workflow ID for use in cache keys.
   383	// It removes all hyphens and converts to lowercase to create a filesystem-safe identifier.
   384	// Example: "Smoke-Copilot" -> "smokecopilot"
   385	func SanitizeWorkflowIDForCacheKey(workflowID string) string {
   386	        // Convert to lowercase
   387	        sanitized := strings.ToLower(workflowID)
   388	        // Remove all hyphens
   389	        sanitized = strings.ReplaceAll(sanitized, "-", "")
   390	        return sanitized

//go:build !integration

package cli

import (
	"math"
	"testing"
	"time"

	"github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/workflow"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
)

func TestDetectTaskDomain(t *testing.T) {
	processedRun := ProcessedRun{
		Run: WorkflowRun{
			WorkflowName: "Weekly Research Report",
			WorkflowPath: ".github/workflows/weekly-research.yml",
			Event:        "schedule",
		},
	}

	domain := detectTaskDomain(processedRun, nil, nil, nil)
	require.NotNil(t, domain, "domain should be detected")
	assert.Equal(t, "research", domain.Name)
	assert.Equal(t, "Research", domain.Label)
}

func TestBuildAgenticAssessmentsFlagsPotentialDeterministicAlternative(t *testing.T) {
	processedRun := ProcessedRun{
		Run: WorkflowRun{
			WorkflowName: "Issue Triage",
			Turns:        2,
			Duration:     2 * time.Minute,
		},
	}
	metrics := MetricsData{Turns: 2}
	toolUsage := []ToolUsageInfo{{Name: "github_issue_read", CallCount: 1}}
	domain := &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "triage", Label: "Triage"}
	fingerprint := &BehaviorFingerprint{
		ExecutionStyle:  "directed",
		ToolBreadth:     "narrow",
		ActuationStyle:  "read_only",
		ResourceProfile: "lean",
		DispatchMode:    "standalone",
	}

	assessments := buildAgenticAssessments(processedRun, metrics, toolUsage, nil, domain, fingerprint, nil)
	require.NotEmpty(t, assessments)
	assert.Equal(t, "overkill_for_agentic", assessments[0].Kind)
}

func TestBuildAgenticAssessmentsFlagsResourceHeavyRun(t *testing.T) {
	processedRun := ProcessedRun{
		Run: WorkflowRun{
			WorkflowName:   "Deep Research",
			Turns:          15,
			Duration:       22 * time.Minute,
			SafeItemsCount: 4,
		},
	}
	metrics := MetricsData{Turns: 15}
	toolUsage := []ToolUsageInfo{
		{Name: "bash", CallCount: 4},
		{Name: "grep", CallCount: 3},
		{Name: "gh", CallCount: 2},
		{Name: "github_issue_read", CallCount: 2},
		{Name: "sed", CallCount: 1},
		{Name: "cat", CallCount: 1},
		{Name: "jq", CallCount: 1},
	}
	domain := &TaskDomainInfo{Name: "research", Label: "Research"}
	fingerprint := buildBehaviorFingerprint(processedRun, metrics, toolUsage, []CreatedItemReport{{Type: "create_issue"}}, nil)

	assessments := buildAgenticAssessments(processedRun, metrics, toolUsage, []CreatedItemReport{{Type: "create_issue"}}, domain, fingerprint, nil)

	var found bool
	for _, assessment := range assessments {
		if assessment.Kind == "resource_heavy_for_domain" {
			found = true
			assert.Equal(t, "high", assessment.Severity)
		}
	}
	assert.True(t, found, "resource heavy assessment should be present")
}

func TestBuildAuditDataIncludesAgenticAnalysis(t *testing.T) {
	processedRun := ProcessedRun{
		Run: WorkflowRun{
			DatabaseID:   7,
			WorkflowName: "Issue Triage",
			WorkflowPath: ".github/workflows/issue-triage.yml",
			Status:       "completed",
			Conclusion:   "success",
			Duration:     3 * time.Minute,
			Turns:        3,
			Event:        "issues",
			LogsPath:     t.TempDir(),
		},
	}
	metrics := LogMetrics{Turns: 3}

	auditData := buildAuditData(processedRun, metrics, nil)
	require.NotNil(t, auditData.TaskDomain, "task domain should be present")
	require.NotNil(t, auditData.BehaviorFingerprint, "behavioral fingerprint should be present")
	assert.NotEmpty(t, auditData.AgenticAssessments, "agentic assessments should be present")
	assert.Equal(t, "triage", auditData.TaskDomain.Name)
}

     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "encoding/json"
     5	        "fmt"
     6	        "os"
     7	        "path/filepath"
     8	        "time"
     9	
    10	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/console"
    11	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/logger"
    12	)
    13	
    14	var logsCacheLog = logger.New("cli:logs_cache")
    15	
    16	// loadRunSummary attempts to load a run summary from disk
    17	// Returns the summary and a boolean indicating if it was successfully loaded and is valid
    18	func loadRunSummary(outputDir string, verbose bool) (*RunSummary, bool) {
    19	        logsCacheLog.Printf("Loading run summary from cache: dir=%s", outputDir)
    20	        summaryPath := filepath.Join(outputDir, runSummaryFileName)
    21	
    22	        // Check if summary file exists
    23	        if _, err := os.Stat(summaryPath); os.IsNotExist(err) {
    24	                logsCacheLog.Print("Run summary cache file does not exist")
    25	                return nil, false
    26	        }
    27	
    28	        // Read the summary file
    29	        data, err := os.ReadFile(summaryPath)
    30	        if err != nil {
    31	                logsCacheLog.Printf("Failed to read run summary cache: %v", err)
    32	                if verbose {
    33	                        fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatWarningMessage(fmt.Sprintf("Failed to read run summary: %v", err)))
    34	                }
    35	                return nil, false
    36	        }
    37	
    38	        // Parse the JSON
    39	        var summary RunSummary
    40	        if err := json.Unmarshal(data, &summary); err != nil {
    41	                logsCacheLog.Printf("Failed to parse run summary JSON: %v", err)
    42	                if verbose {
    43	                        fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatWarningMessage(fmt.Sprintf("Failed to parse run summary: %v", err)))
    44	                }
    45	                return nil, false
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        // Validate CLI version matches
    49	        currentVersion := GetVersion()
    50	        if summary.CLIVersion != currentVersion {
    51	                logsCacheLog.Printf("CLI version mismatch: cached=%s, current=%s", summary.CLIVersion, currentVersion)
    52	                if verbose {
    53	                        fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatInfoMessage(fmt.Sprintf("Run summary version mismatch (cached: %s, current: %s), will reprocess", summary.CLIVersion, currentVersion)))
    54	                }
    55	                return nil, false
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        logsCacheLog.Printf("Successfully loaded cached run summary: run_id=%d", summary.RunID)
    59	        if verbose {
    60	                fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatInfoMessage(fmt.Sprintf("Loaded cached run summary for run %d (processed at %s)", summary.RunID, summary.ProcessedAt.Format(time.RFC3339))))
    61	        }
    62	
    63	        return &summary, true
    64	}
    65	
    66	// saveRunSummary saves a run summary to disk
    67	func saveRunSummary(outputDir string, summary *RunSummary, verbose bool) error {
    68	        logsCacheLog.Printf("Saving run summary to cache: dir=%s, run_id=%d", outputDir, summary.RunID)
    69	        summaryPath := filepath.Join(outputDir, runSummaryFileName)
    70	
    71	        // Marshal to JSON with indentation for readability
    72	        data, err := json.MarshalIndent(summary, "", "  ")
    73	        if err != nil {
    74	                logsCacheLog.Printf("Failed to marshal run summary: %v", err)
    75	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to marshal run summary: %w", err)
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        // Write to file
    79	        if err := os.WriteFile(summaryPath, data, 0644); err != nil {
    80	                logsCacheLog.Printf("Failed to write run summary to disk: %v", err)
    81	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to write run summary: %w", err)
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        logsCacheLog.Printf("Successfully saved run summary cache: path=%s", summaryPath)
    85	        if verbose {
    86	                fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatInfoMessage("Saved run summary to "+summaryPath))
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        return nil
    90	}

   259	func TestBuildToolUsageInfoAggregatesAndSorts(t *testing.T) {
   260	        metrics := LogMetrics{
   261	                ToolCalls: []workflow.ToolCallInfo{
   262	                        {Name: "bash", CallCount: 3, MaxInputSize: 100, MaxOutputSize: 200, MaxDuration: 1 * time.Second},
   263	                        {Name: "github_issue_read", CallCount: 5, MaxInputSize: 50, MaxOutputSize: 300, MaxDuration: 500 * time.Millisecond},
   264	                        {Name: "bash", CallCount: 2, MaxInputSize: 150, MaxOutputSize: 180, MaxDuration: 2 * time.Second},
   265	                },
   266	        }
   267	
   268	        result := buildToolUsageInfo(metrics)
   269	
   270	        require.Len(t, result, 2, "duplicate tool names should be merged")
   271	
   272	        // bash has CallCount 3+2=5 (merged), github_issue_read has CallCount 5.
   273	        // Both have equal call counts, so the tie is broken alphabetically: "bash" < "github_issue_read".
   274	        assert.Equal(t, "bash", result[0].Name, "alphabetically first among equal call counts should be first")
   275	        assert.Equal(t, 5, result[0].CallCount, "bash call counts should be summed: 3+2=5")
   276	        assert.Equal(t, 150, result[0].MaxInputSize, "max input size should be max across merged entries")
   277	        assert.Equal(t, 200, result[0].MaxOutputSize, "max output size should be max across merged entries")
   278	        assert.NotEmpty(t, result[0].MaxDuration, "max duration should be set from the longest call")
   279	
   280	        assert.Equal(t, "github_issue_read", result[1].Name, "alphabetically second should be second")
   281	        assert.Equal(t, 5, result[1].CallCount, "call count for github_issue_read should be 5")
   282	}

//go:build !integration

package cli

import (
    "strings"
    "testing"
)

func TestReproMCPToolUsageFeedsAgenticToolTypes(t *testing.T) {
    processedRun := ProcessedRun{Run: WorkflowRun{DatabaseID: 24493327785, WorkflowName: "Copilot PR Prompt Pattern Analysis", Status: "completed", Conclusion: "success", Turns: 20, LogsPath: t.TempDir()}}
    metrics := LogMetrics{Turns: 20}
    mcpData := &MCPToolUsageData{Summary: []MCPToolSummary{
        {ServerName: "safeoutputs", ToolName: "create_discussion", CallCount: 1},
        {ServerName: "safeoutputs", ToolName: "push_repo_memory", CallCount: 2},
    }}

    auditData := buildAuditData(processedRun, metrics, mcpData)
    if len(auditData.ToolUsage) != 2 {
        t.Fatalf("tool usage should fall back to distinct MCP tools; got %d: %#v", len(auditData.ToolUsage), auditData.ToolUsage)
    }
    if auditData.BehaviorFingerprint == nil || auditData.BehaviorFingerprint.ToolBreadth != "moderate" {
        t.Fatalf("behavior fingerprint should use MCP tools for breadth; got %#v", auditData.BehaviorFingerprint)
    }
    if len(auditData.ObservabilityInsights) == 0 || strings.Contains(auditData.ObservabilityInsights[0].Summary, "0 tool types") {
        t.Fatalf("observability should not report 0 tool types; got %#v", auditData.ObservabilityInsights)
    }
}
GOEOF
trap '"'"'rm -f pkg/cli/repro_mcp_tool_types_tmp_test.go'"'"' EXIT
go test ./pkg/cli -run TestReproMCPToolUsageFeedsAgenticToolTypes -count=1
'

   539	// extractPreAgentStepErrors scans workflow step log files for failure content when the
   540	// agent never executed (no agent-stdio.log present). This surfaces errors from pre-agent
   541	// steps such as lockdown validation, binary installation, or repository checkout failures.
   542	//
   543	// Step log files are stored in workflow-logs/{job}/{step_num}_{step_name}.txt after
   544	// downloading via downloadWorkflowRunLogs. The function first scans all step logs for
   545	// ##[error] annotations (GitHub Actions error annotations), which are the most precise
   546	// failure indicators. If none are found, it falls back to the content of the last step
   547	// (highest step number) as a general failure indicator.
   548	func extractPreAgentStepErrors(logsPath string) []ErrorInfo {
   549	        // If agent-stdio.log exists, the agent ran - don't scan step logs
   550	        agentStdioPath := filepath.Join(logsPath, "agent-stdio.log")
   551	        if _, err := os.Stat(agentStdioPath); err == nil {
   552	                auditReportLog.Printf("agent-stdio.log found, skipping pre-agent step error extraction")
   553	                return nil
   554	        }
   555	
   556	        // Look for step log files in workflow-logs subdirectory
   557	        workflowLogsDir := filepath.Join(logsPath, "workflow-logs")
   558	        if _, err := os.Stat(workflowLogsDir); err != nil {
   559	                auditReportLog.Printf("workflow-logs directory not found, skipping step log extraction")
   560	                return nil

    48	func buildToolUsageInfoWithMCP(metrics LogMetrics, mcpToolUsage *MCPToolUsageData) []ToolUsageInfo {
    49	        toolStats := make(map[string]*ToolUsageInfo)
    50	
    51	        for _, toolCall := range metrics.ToolCalls {
    52	                displayKey := workflow.PrettifyToolName(toolCall.Name)
    53	                if existing, exists := toolStats[displayKey]; exists {
    54	                        existing.CallCount += toolCall.CallCount
    55	                        if toolCall.MaxInputSize > existing.MaxInputSize {
    56	                                existing.MaxInputSize = toolCall.MaxInputSize
    57	                        }
    58	                        if toolCall.MaxOutputSize > existing.MaxOutputSize {
    59	                                existing.MaxOutputSize = toolCall.MaxOutputSize
    60	                        }
    61	                        if toolCall.MaxDuration > 0 {
    62	                                maxDuration := timeutil.FormatDuration(toolCall.MaxDuration)
    63	                                if existing.MaxDuration == "" || toolCall.MaxDuration > parseDurationString(existing.MaxDuration) {
    64	                                        existing.MaxDuration = maxDuration
    65	                                }
    66	                        }
    67	                        continue
    68	                }
    69	
    70	                info := &ToolUsageInfo{
    71	                        Name:          displayKey,
    72	                        CallCount:     toolCall.CallCount,
    73	                        MaxInputSize:  toolCall.MaxInputSize,
    74	                        MaxOutputSize: toolCall.MaxOutputSize,
    75	                }
    76	                if toolCall.MaxDuration > 0 {
    77	                        info.MaxDuration = timeutil.FormatDuration(toolCall.MaxDuration)
    78	                }
    79	                toolStats[displayKey] = info
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        toolUsage := make([]ToolUsageInfo, 0, len(toolStats))
    83	        for _, info := range toolStats {
    84	                toolUsage = append(toolUsage, *info)
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        slices.SortFunc(toolUsage, func(a, b ToolUsageInfo) int {
    88	                if a.CallCount != b.CallCount {
    89	                        return b.CallCount - a.CallCount
    90	                }

    48	func buildToolUsageInfoWithMCP(metrics LogMetrics, mcpToolUsage *MCPToolUsageData) []ToolUsageInfo {
    49	        toolStats := make(map[string]*ToolUsageInfo)
    50	
    51	        for _, toolCall := range metrics.ToolCalls {
    52	                displayKey := workflow.PrettifyToolName(toolCall.Name)
    53	                if existing, exists := toolStats[displayKey]; exists {
    54	                        existing.CallCount += toolCall.CallCount
    55	                        if toolCall.MaxInputSize > existing.MaxInputSize {
    56	                                existing.MaxInputSize = toolCall.MaxInputSize
    57	                        }
    58	                        if toolCall.MaxOutputSize > existing.MaxOutputSize {
    59	                                existing.MaxOutputSize = toolCall.MaxOutputSize
    60	                        }
    61	                        if toolCall.MaxDuration > 0 {
    62	                                maxDuration := timeutil.FormatDuration(toolCall.MaxDuration)
    63	                                if existing.MaxDuration == "" || toolCall.MaxDuration > parseDurationString(existing.MaxDuration) {
    64	                                        existing.MaxDuration = maxDuration
    65	                                }
    66	                        }
    67	                        continue
    68	                }
    69	
    70	                info := &ToolUsageInfo{
    71	                        Name:          displayKey,
    72	                        CallCount:     toolCall.CallCount,
    73	                        MaxInputSize:  toolCall.MaxInputSize,
    74	                        MaxOutputSize: toolCall.MaxOutputSize,
    75	                }
    76	                if toolCall.MaxDuration > 0 {
    77	                        info.MaxDuration = timeutil.FormatDuration(toolCall.MaxDuration)
    78	                }
    79	                toolStats[displayKey] = info
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        addMCPTool := func(serverName, toolName string, callCount, maxInputSize, maxOutputSize int, maxDuration string) {
    83	                name := formatMCPToolUsageName(serverName, toolName)
    84	                if name == "" {
    85	                        return
    86	                }
    87	                if callCount <= 0 {
    88	                        callCount = 1
    89	                }
    90	                if existing, exists := toolStats[name]; exists {
    91	                        existing.CallCount += callCount
    92	                        if maxInputSize > existing.MaxInputSize {
    93	                                existing.MaxInputSize = maxInputSize
    94	                        }
    95	                        if maxOutputSize > existing.MaxOutputSize {
    96	                                existing.MaxOutputSize = maxOutputSize
    97	                        }
    98	                        if maxDuration != "" && (existing.MaxDuration == "" || parseDurationString(maxDuration) > parseDurationString(existing.MaxDuration)) {
    99	                                existing.MaxDuration = maxDuration
   100	                        }
   101	                        return
   102	                }
   103	                toolStats[name] = &ToolUsageInfo{
   104	                        Name:          name,
   105	                        CallCount:     callCount,
   106	                        MaxInputSize:  maxInputSize,
   107	                        MaxOutputSize: maxOutputSize,
   108	                        MaxDuration:   maxDuration,
   109	                }
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        if mcpToolUsage != nil {
   113	                for _, summary := range mcpToolUsage.Summary {
   114	                        addMCPTool(summary.ServerName, summary.ToolName, summary.CallCount, summary.MaxInputSize, summary.MaxOutputSize, summary.MaxDuration)
   115	                }
   116	                for _, call := range mcpToolUsage.ToolCalls {
   117	                        addMCPTool(call.ServerName, call.ToolName, 1, call.InputSize, call.OutputSize, call.Duration)
   118	                }
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        toolUsage := make([]ToolUsageInfo, 0, len(toolStats))
   122	        for _, info := range toolStats {
   123	                toolUsage = append(toolUsage, *info)
   124	        }
   125	
   126	        slices.SortFunc(toolUsage, func(a, b ToolUsageInfo) int {
   127	                if a.CallCount != b.CallCount {
   128	                        return b.CallCount - a.CallCount
   129	                }
   130	                return strings.Compare(a.Name, b.Name)
   131	        })
   132	
   133	        return toolUsage
   134	}
